I've taken a look at Els's doodle poll (thanks, Els!). I'd like to suggest Tuesday, September 15, 8am, or Thursday, September 17. 8am EDT (GMT -4).  I have a slight preference for Tuesday, but let me know what your thoughts are.

Should we ask that a representative from the early stage researchers group come? Since we are deciding roles for the board, it's probably not necessary for everyone in that group to be there, but it might be good to have one representative there. I'm cc'ing Jamie for his thoughts.

Also, I would like to try a video meeting. Does anyone object? If we do a video meeting, someone would need to take minutes. Volunteers if so?
